***блокадный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блокадный.html>блока́дный</a> (16906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blokáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокадный.html>блока́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blokádnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> under siege, blockade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блокадный.html>блока́дный</a></b> ленингра́д</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blokádnyj</b> Leningrád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Leningrad under siege</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blockade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> block; blocking; obstruction</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">under siege</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадный.html>оса́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osadnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">siege</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blokáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осада.html>оса́да</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>штурм</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šturm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***блокировка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вка</a> (26095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировать.html>блоки́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blokírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blokiróvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blocking, block, blockage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lock</li></ol>

***блокирующий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блокирующий.html>блоки́рующий</a> (10084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***блоха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a> (11916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blъxa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰluseh₂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bloxá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блохи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>бло́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>бло́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аркан.html>арка́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá v karmáne <b>bloxá</b> na arkáne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m flat broke.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">I have a <b>flea</b> on a lasso in my pocket.</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***блуд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a> (32131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">блꙋдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bludŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blǫdъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰlendʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blud</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блу́да</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>licentiousness, lechery, fornication</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блудить.html>блуди́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bludítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блудный.html>блу́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blúdnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блудница.html>блудни́ца</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bludníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***блудить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блудить.html>блуди́ть</a> (29759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">блѫдити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blǫditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блудить.html>блуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bludítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat  dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wander, to roam</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блудить.html>блуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bludítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to fornicate, to whore around</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блудный.html>блу́дный</a> (19986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>prodigal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блудный.html>блу́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сын</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blúdnyj</b> syn</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>prodigal</b> son</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lascivious, lecherous</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bluždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to roam, to wander, to rove, to ramble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bluždátʹ</b> po svétu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rove/roam about the world</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ющий</a> (15394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bluždájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bluždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bluždájuščij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>constantly changing location or direction of movement; wandering <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a light</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>shifting <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a look or glance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>intermittent, appearing and disappearing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ющий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонек.html>огонёк</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bluždájuščij</b> ogonjók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">will o' the wisp, ignis fatuus</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>intermittent</b> light</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wandering <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">abnormally mobile</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждающий.html>блужда́ющая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почка.html>по́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bluždájuščaja</b> póčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>wandering</b> kidney</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***блуза.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блуза.html>блу́за</a> (23499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">blouse</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bluse</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуза.html>блу́за</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blúza</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуза.html>блу́зы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуза.html>блу́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуза.html>блуз</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blouse (usually a working blouse)</li></ol>

***блюдо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a> (3126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bľudo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bljúdo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блюд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dish, plate</li>
<li>dish, course
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вятся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицы</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne nrávjatsja <b>bljúda</b> iz kúricy!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I like chicken!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***блюсти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a> (18478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bľusti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*bjaustei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰewdʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bljustí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюсти.html>соблюсти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to guard, to keep
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> zakóny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to observe the laws; abide by the laws</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> interésy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to watch over the interests</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to guard one's chastity; 2) to watch one's waistline; keep in shape</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***бог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> (254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bogъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">box</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бого́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богиня.html>боги́ня</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>God</li>
<li>god, idol
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>box</b> jevó znájet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God only knows!; goodness knows!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bóže moj!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">oh God!; good gracious!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>box</b> s nim!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Forget him!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">daj <b>box</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God willing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ей-бо́гу!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jej-bógu!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">really!; really and truly!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́га</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rádi <b>bóga</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for God’s sake!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сохранить.html>сохрани́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́же</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soxraní bóže!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">save oh Lord!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́гу</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sláva bógu!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">glory to God!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Usually not capitalized in Russian in the sense of idol, or when referring to a single god with a polytheistic pantheon. It is normally capitalized in monotheistic sense, such as in Islamic or Christian discourse (see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Box</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), except for some common set expressions<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.</li></ul>
